- 2 nd   1991  3. 28 -  3. 30
- 3 rd   1991  6.  6 - 6.   7

results are met the limits of noise level stated in table 5.2.6 -   4.    And
at St. N-3 where is 4 km far from project site, noise level ( at street &
port side ) has analyzed in the range of 48 dB(A) - 50 dB(A) in the daytime
which is below the limits of noise level, therefore,   it  is  predicted   to
exist no specific sources of noise around the project site.

A state sensible to the most man and have a window

B. Environmental Impact by Project
In general, noise and vibration produced by this project can be
divided  into  the  condition  under  project   construction   and   project
operation. Under operating condition, it is expected that vessel traffic
is not frequent at the receiving terminal and no equipments producing noise
inside LNG      receiving   terminal,  therefore,  noise   & vibration during
construction process has predicted in this section.
1. Noise
Major noise sources due to commited construction equipment are dump
truck, bull dozer, back hoe etc., and noise impacts from the site to
circumferencial area due to construction equipment operation has considered
as source of hemispherical sound wave, then, noise level by distance has
been predicted.
Prediction of noise level is calculated based on the following
equation. Type, no.s and noise level of commited construction equipment are
described in table 5.2.6 -8.

Based on the impact prediction resuLts about circ umferencial area on
construction work, isolated distance etc, as above, it is anticipated
that, in the process of offshore works such as dredging & marine facility
construction, noise  pollution is not generated since     construction  site
is approximately 3km away from residential area.   In the process of onshore
works such as causeway & revetment construction, highest noise level which
is produced by causeway construction is in excess of 75 dB(A), noise level
limit of class I & II district due to construction equipment,for area with-
in about 200m from causeway.
Therefore, mitigation measures should be established for the places
expecting short period of noise pollution like partial area of Shin-chon
village of Dong-choon dong, Nam koo, Incheon city.
2. Vibration
It is defined that vibration is a strong shaking which generated from
the operation of machinery and tools.( Noise & Vibration regulations, para.
2 of clause  2   )     Vibrations   to  be produced   due  to  this  project
construction will be caused   by the heavy construction equipment  operation
and sources of vibration are classified as follows.
- Instantaneous shock by diesel hammer etc.,
- Continuous shock by compressor etc.,
- Vibration by vehicle traffic
Thus, a shock wave is produced by shocks given from construction
equipment    and then, vibration is generated by transfering a   shock  wave
to the ground. Vibration intensity by construction equipment and isolated
distance is     decribed in table 5.2.6 - 11.

In fact, vibration regulations to be applied for construction site in
the  country   is  not   provided,   therefore,  vibration    regulations    for
individual construction works of Japan has been applied for this project.
In  conclusion,   it   is  evaluated   that  vibration   impact  due    to
construction      equipment is not significant, since vibration level      at   a
distance of 20 m       from bull dozer is about 75 dB which     is  satisfactory
to Japanese regulation as presented in table 5.2.6 - 12.

Note; (1) Districts described below are class I districts.
- Districts try to maintain a excellent living condition.
- Districts have a need to be silent for a living.

however, prevent vibration because of the greater occupancy
of residents.
- Districts near hospital, school.
(2) Class II districts is the exception of class I, where should
maintain a living condition for resident.
C. Method for Reducing the Baneful Impact
It is required to establish an effective measures for noise polltion
produced by construction equipment not to give impact on near residential
area and it is expected that installation of soundproof facilities is more
effective than  the   interception  of  soundtransfer,   since  construction
equipment is moving according to their usage.
Thus, noise to be produced during the process of construction will be
minimized considering following measures.
- Confine working time to a daytime 06:00 - 18:00 as far as possible.
- Set speedlimit of construction vehicle to 20 km/hr.
- Effective commitment of equipment by construction work.
- Install a sound arrester on each equipment.
- Inform blasting works to neighbors before operation.
Futhermore, by installing a temporary soundproof facility to intercept
a wave, mitigation effect can be obtained for causeway construction and
noise reduction level can be calculated as below.

5.2.8 Leisure and Scenery
A. Present Environment Condition
1. Leisure
No leisure facilities are exist in this project site because project
site is located about 7 km far from the coast and leisure facilities status
of Incheon city to where project site belongs are 177 places which
comprises 9 places of natural park, 53 places of vicinity park, one park
cemetry ,111 places of children's park and 3 places of amusement park and
area of 32,432,550 n? totally as described in table 5.2.8 - 1.

Reference: Statistical year book of Incheon, 1990
Also, :r'- national marine tourist resort development plan as the only
harbour city for a national capital is being expedited around Young-jong
island and Young-yoo island newly incorporated.
On the other hands, representative leisure facilities of Incheon city
are Song island, Wol-mi island, New Incheon amusement park, Soo-bong park,
Freedom park etc., and status of facilities are as follows.
a) Song island Amusement Park
It is situated at the location with Cheong-ryang Mt., 6 km far from
Incheon city to south, for a background near West Sea.The park is furnished
with artificial swimming beach installed newly in 1963, swimming pool, boat
launching station, athletic field and several recreation facilities and
furthermore, there are Neung-hur dae, 1-leung-reun temple, memorial building
to Incheon landing operaion in the vicinity and a small island, a-am do, is
being made a scenery there a magnificent sight.



The park which is developed with modernized facilities are managed as
a general amusement park by Incheon city tour co. Ltd, and it is possible
for swimming beach resort to control water level by a sluice and very
crowded with peoples from Seoul and other city in summer because of thicker
smooth sand laying at sea bottom.
b)   Wol-mi island
Wol-mi island is a maritime city having an about 4 km circumference
which is 1 km west far away from Incheon station and it is connected to
reclamation area nowadays.For a long time, it is known as an amusement park
and therefore, Incheon reminds Wol-mi island first.   Wol-mi island, symbol
of Incheon city, is beloved by foreigners under the name of ROSE at the end
of Cho-sun are now reclamated completely and 20 m wide roads & factories
besides of streets are constructed and thus, it is remained a mere shadow
of its former prosperity.
Before Independence, it had been satisfied all the requisites of an
amusement place by furnishing swimming beach resort, kisaeng house, a zoo
and botanical gardens.       The park has ever  been  openned   to  all  the
peoples for a while after Independence, but now, only a few old men are
keeping its nostalgia ever since all the facilities are destroyed due to
Korean war.
Also, this is the historical place of Yi dynasty where a fort and a
castle had been constructed at that time and there is an episode that
Hwa-bang-yi-zil, minister of Japan, had escaped secretly to Wol-mi island,
Incheon and return to his country by bording naval vessel of Britain at the
Im-o Military Revolt of 1882.
Wol-mi island is the first and the most westernized island taking
Bengin and Sinmi history event as a momentum and there is nothing to be
desired to enjoy romance of the sea, for instance, scenery of sunset with
smell of the sea, tasty of fresh rawfish watching West Sea under beautiful
moonlight, entertainment from the aroma of coffee with a magnificent sight
through a clear glass and sea traveling.
c) New Amusement Park of Incheon
New park which is located at middle of the way from downtown of
Incheon to Song island is furnishing filtrated clean and fresh water from
3.3 X 105 m2 reservoir for swimming resort, thus, keeping clear sea water
and retaining enormous facilities for adults, children, babies etc,.
d) Soo-bong Park
There are Buddhist temples such  as  Soo-bong  am,  Cheong-ryoung   sa,
Moon-hwa sa etc., and an arbour named Moo-deuck jeong.Moreover, a   monument
cherishing and praise to the war dead of Incheon birth has been installed
at Oct. 5, 1972 and an anti-Communist center is placed at the top and it is
being intoxicated with victory through the war record monument of Incheon
to commemorate Landing operation of Incheon and the monument to students
soldier's entry of Korean resident in Japan in the war as a model of
patriotism by cherishing the loyal dead during Korean war.
-.382-



Thus, Soo-bong park is highlighted as an family entertainment place
equiped with various kinds of leisure facilities such as a children's
pleasure resort, a promenade, atheletic facilities and a rest area etc.
e) Freedom Park
Freedom park is consist of overall Ueng-bong Mt. at the downtown area
of Incheon city and originally, it has been called as Universal park or
Western park because the park is managed by the foreigner settlement
corporation after the opening of Incheon harbour and management & controll
of the park transfered to Incheon city in 1941 with the abolition of
foreign dwelling. A bronze statue of General Maccarther, the man who bring
a come-from-behind victory of war by enforcing Incheon landing operation,is
set up and Youn-o jeong & Seuck-cheung soo showing a fantastic beauty of
classical architecture is located on the hill towards Wol-mi island and a
view of whole Incheon city and harbour can be gotten and it is suitable for
promenade either and sculptures of the ministers participated in the treaty
of amity and a monument to celebrate 100th anniversary of Korea-America
ammity has been installed.

2. Scenery
The project site is surrounded by Moo-uei island, Young-you island to
west and by Incheon harbour to northeast and by Dae-boo island to south
etc., and a slime is formed around project site at the ebb tide due to high
tidal range and hence, it is a classical tidal land of harbour area with a
beautiful scenery of a great many blacktailed guills' flying. However,
particular element of beautiful scenery does not exist around the project
site, since it is located on the sea.
B. Environmental Impact by Project
1. Leisure
As prescribed above, there are no particular or artificial leisure
facilities around the project site at the present, however, it is planning
to provide athletic fields( 21,600 nt ) and exhibition hall( 31,800 ne ) at
the southern area of the project site for relax and leisure of employee.
2. Scenery
By constructing several structures such as LNG tank for this project,
vertical element of scenery will be raised more than horizontal element of
scenery, however, no impacts to the scenery are anticipated because they
are very far separated from island or coast of Incheon city.

B. Environmental Impact by Project
In this chapter, impacts affect human body, which are generated from
diffusion and combustion of gas, has been determined only, since it is
presummed that no impacts to sanitation and public health will not be
produced owing to the performance of this project.
- :388 -



1. Diffusion of Gas
LNG turns into liquids at an ultra low temperature of -162 oC under
atmospheric pressure and LNG will evaporate pretty soon taking conduction
heat from ground surface, convection heat from the air, radiation heat from
the sun in the case that LNG which evaporate continuously by absorbing
heats aruond circumference in the reservoir efflulx to the ground surface in
the normal temperature.      Evaporated gas will compose white  gas  clouds
in the air and diffuse along wind direction by condensation of water
particle in the air.
On the other hands, effusion, evaporation, diffusion and fire-fighting
characteristics of gas are continuously under research as stated in table
5.2.9 - 5 and liquids surface expansion, shape of evaporation and status of
diffusion and effusion are described for the each case that LNG is effused
on the sea and effused to ground surface from underground reservoir and
about underground reservoir tank for LNG.
a)   Expansion  of Liquids   Effused Plane
(1)   Effusion  to  Land
Generally, LNG reservoir have a liquids collection pit in the
liquids protector embankment for the purpose of preventing expansion of
liquids leakage at the connected piping to reservoir.In this case, it
doesn't matter to assumme that liquids are keeping constant depth like
collection pit of on-land reservoir, whereas effused liquids are to be
gathered into collection pit in the case of clogging of piping at pump
barrel for underground reservoir.
(2)   Effusion  to  Sea
For the case of effusion of LNG to sea due to damage of unloading
arm etc, an emergency intercepter will be equipped at both of vessel side
and loading platform side and also emergency loading interception system
has been established for any emergency case.For instance, effused LNG at
any reason will expand until all LNG evaporate by taking heats on seawater.

b) Evaporation Velocity
(1) Effusion to Land
LNG effused to land shows an abnormal evaporation at initial time by
taking heats from ground surface and return to stable condition as ground
getting  cool   and  finally,  normal  evaporation   is  presented   at   the
equilibrium condition of potential heat and admission heat from outside.
Evaporation speed( falling speed of liquids plane ) of LNG effuse to
land varies dependent upon water content of ground surface, grain size of
soil particle and mixing ratio of stone and turns to stable condition of
0.5 mm/min. of evaporation speed obtained from J.G.A, AGA, Gas.De.France
after a long time has been passed.
(2) Effusion to the sea
LNG will evaporate mainly taking heats from seawater after effused
normally. Based on the study report of American bureau of mining about
effusion to the sea,.LNG will evaporate with a speed of 25.4 mm/min. (
constant evaporation speed V ) taking heats of seawater gradually at
unlimited water surface.

c) Diffusion
When leaked LNG not ignited will diffuse in air, it will expand and
diffuse in low air, since gas right after leakage is low in temperature and
heavier than air in the outskirts.For fire fighting purpose, it is
extremely important to predict the range of lowest limit concentration of
gas combustion.
It is hard to predict development of gas diffusion because gas
diffusion depends mainly on meteorological condition such as temperature,
wind speed, humidity and topographic condition and capacity of heat etc.,
however, the phenomenon is well defined at present by a great many test on
diffusion from many countries.
2. Combustion
a)   Characteristics  of  Natural  Gas  Combustion
LNG receiving terminal facilities have been designed not to penetrate
leaked gas into enclosed space such as inside of building, office
considering the point that leaked natural gas may have a fire break out due
to an ignition source.    And air permeation will not be taken place by the
reason that constant pressure of reservoir tank inside is maintained and
controlled a little higher than atmospheric pressure by boil off gas.
-392 -



Ignition of LNG clouds transfer flame smoothly and comprise dispersed
yellowish red colour flame combustion at a combustion speed of 10 mm/min. (
falling speed of liquids plane ).      Also, state of LNG gas white   clouds
represents the result of water particle condensation in the air owing to
its low temperature and 5 % of lowest limit concentration of gas combustion
is within LNG gas white clouds. As above, it is the characteristics of LNG
evaporated gas to define safety range clearly in the case of leakage.
Intensity of LNG flame ( radial emission capacity ) is about 50,000 -
65,000 Kcal/ne..h which is somewhat higher than 50,000 Kcal/m .h of gasoline
and about 36,000 Kcal/mr .h of crude oil as described in table 5.2.9 - 6 and
therefore, effects to the vicinity in case of fire shall be considered
carefully  more  than  gasoline  combustion.Combustion   speed  and   radial
emission capacity of LNG has been shown at table 5.2.9 - 7 attained from
test results of table 5.2.9 - 6.

and 240 ft distance to heat receiving point.
b) Impacts by Radiation Heat
(1) Impacts to Human Body
It is known that all organisms including human being are benefited to
radiation heat from sun and are familiar with radiation heat from heating
equipment such as artificial infrared heater.       However, radiation heat
for human body is too high then it may bring a serious burn cause blisters
on the skin and even reach to death not limited to light degree of burn as
stated in table 5.2.9 -  8.      Accordingly,  a  countermeasure   shall  be
established by predicting radiation heat in case of LNG facilities in fire
at any case.

of LNG  receiving   terminal  and     it  is  important  to  grasp  critical
intensity of radiation heat simultaneously.      Also,  it  is  required  to
provide a fireproof structure and springkler facility for the places where
a possibility exist to deform their shape due to compulsory radiation heat.
Critical intensity of radiation heat for inflammables has been stated in
table 5.2.9 - 12.

C. Method for Reducing the Baneful Impact
1. Facilities for Emergency
a) Early Detection of Emergency
It is desirable to establish early detection system of- emergency by
install inflammable gas detector, low temperature detector and high
temperature detector for fire to find possible accidents such as LNG
leakage as soon as possible.
For above, following equipments are required to be installed.
(1) Gas Leakage Detection and Alarm System
This is to be installed at the circumfernee of LNG tank, loading arm
equipment and pump facilities for early detection of gas leakage, and
contact type and semi-conductor type are utilized.25 % of lowest limit
explosion is the standard for alarm level.
(2) Low Temperature Detection and Alarm System
For early detection of LNG effusion, it may be installed at
collection pit inside liquids protection bank of tank on land and at sump
to  complement  gas    leakage   detector.      Gas   expansion   type   and
thermoelectric type are utilized.
(3) Fire Detector and Alarm System
It is installed for detection of fire and alarm for high temperature
detection by thermoelectricity which is utilized generally.
b) Facilities for Post Emergency Treatment
Emegency effusion of LNG at any time is inherent problem of LNG
receiving terminal   in nature.       In this   case,  a  cOountermeasure to
minimize effusion quantity is required.    At tank, liquids shoud be removed
to safe place in early stage and simultaneously it is requested to block
leaked point and enough liquids protection bank, high foamy effluence
equipment and evaporation control equipment should be installed for
enormous quantity of effusion.A fixed type of powdered fire extinguisher is
installed at the tank and in many cases, a high foamy effluence fire
extinguisher is installed together for ground tanks'.
Basically, above is effective for piping equipment as exactly same as
tank but block division by valve is more effective.     It  is  required  to
prepare fire-fighting facilities to control and extinguish fire take placed
by effused liquids and gas and powdered fire extinguisher is the most
effective for fire due to LNG.
To minimize critical area on land when LNG effused to ground surface,
it is recommendable to drive gas diffused in vertically and water curtain
equipment is  used  for  above.        These   are  primary  post  treatment
activity of emergence occurrence.
-397-



The first activity to be done of secondary post treatment is to
protect facilities in the vicinity from high tempreature.    In other words,
a measure to protect facilities in the vicinity from radiation heat in case
of fire and heat resistant treatment such as springkling for cooling has
been specified in law  for  tanks.     Also,   it  is required   to  install
sprinklers at the specific places for cooling facilities and equipments in
the  vicinity.      Moreover,  to  preserve  provisions  from   heats   more
effectively, fixed springking system for cooling and heat resistant coating
can be used.
The second thing to be done is to protect facilities in the vicinity
from low temperature.   Normally carbon steel is utilized for roof of tank,
pipe rack structure and temporary structure and therefore, protect cover
which made of materials without brittleness in low temperature shall be
installed on it to prevent brittleness in low temperature by freezing shock
in case of LNG effusion.    Major facilities for treatment are described as
below.
(1) Water Curtain Facilities
Water curtain has both effect of upward diffusion acceleration of
evaporated  gas  and   interception  of   radiation   heat    at   ignition.
Generally it is installed at the circumference of tank, outside of liquids
protection bank and loading equipment.     Capacity can be predicted by the
ability of radiation heat interception and horizontal diffusion prevention
of evaporated gas, and generally 100 - 200 I/min/m is   used  and  depth  of
water curtain, water quantity, type of nozzle can be concluded from it.
(2) High Foamy Effluence Facilities
High foamy facilities are to extinguish fire on the surface of LNG
with high foam liquids of 400 - 500  times  and    this  will  be  installed
inside of liquids protection  bank  of  ground  tank  and    high   foam  is
effective for  evaporated  gas  control.        Foamy  equipment  which  can
totally cover liquids protector bank shoud be selected and netfence may be
installed on liquids protector bank to prevent dispersion of foam.
(3) Powdered Fire Extinguish Facilities
In many LNG receiving terminals, powdered fire extinguish equipments
are installed because it is the most effective for extinguish of LNG
fire. Generally, fixed type is used for tanks, loading equipment etc., and
it is desirable to install 0.34 kg/nt X 30 s capacity   of  nozzle   and  10
kg/m2 of reserve capacity is standard.
(4) Sprinkling Facilities
Springkling facilities system is equipped and installed for the fire
of circumferencial equipment.    In a tank, springkling ring   for  2 or   4
partition is installed in it and normally springkling capacity of 2 - 3
l/min/m7 is used and seawater is used generally  for  springkling.     Fixed
type of springkling facilities ( about 2 I/min/n ) are prepared for the
structures other than tanks,e.g, piping around and pipe rack and fire plugs
which has a springkling capacity of 350 - 450 1/min are installed with a
spacing of 30 - 70 m.
-398-



(5) General Fire Protection System
General fire protection system is that equipped with control
facilities to extinguish fire in early stage and transfer collected data of
fire protection and accidents precisely for coping and monitoring at
control center etc.    There  are   a blanket   alarm display   function  by
facilities and a answer back function and opcniiig and closing operation of
each  emegency   interception  valve  as option   in  this  system.     Main
facilities have been described as below, however, prescribed inflammable
gas detector, low temperature detector and high temperature detector have
not been mentioned.
(a)   abnormality  detector,  inflammable  gas  detector,  high    and   low
temperature
detector : described in previous chapter
(b) Monitoring facility ( indutrial 'V )
It should be equipped to monitor overall area where tanks are to be
installed.
(c) Emergency communication system
-   To  secure  communication  network   in emergency,   paging  phone,
subscribed phone, exclusive phone and wireless phone should be equipped
between the area where tanks to be installed and central control &
instrumentation room.
-   A  warning  signal or    internal  broadcasting  system  should  be
installed to cover all area for notifying of emergency.
(d) Signal transformation system
Detected signals cannot be used for alarm and warning signal
directly because the most of the equipments are fabricated for the
detection in analogue and therefore, signal transformation equipment or
alarm equipment shall be installed.Also, because all these informations are
obtained by marks, a micro computer by multiple marks treatment is utilized
and information transfering is normally done by one cable.       And  it  is
reqired to make possible operation of minimal information if computer is
down.
(e) Control facilities for safety plan in early stage
(f) Emergency interception valve
- To intercept tank and other facilities in emergency, interception
valve should be installed around piping at tank.
- Interception valve should be manual or remote controlled.
- Interception valve at LNG piping should be operated by remote control
and high liquids level detector and alarm system should be installed
to prevent overflow. When the alarm is operated, interception valve
should be operated simultaneousLy.
- Opening and closing operation should be simple, secure and swift.
-  Remote opening and closing operation shoud be possible in the case of
interruption of electric after calamity such as earthquake etc.
-399-



(g) Fire fighting facilities control
- Powdered fire extinguisher ejection valve : remote control or manual
control for operation stop make possible.
- Water curtain facilities : remote control or manual control of
sprinking facilities make possible.
(h) Others
It is desirable to exhibit as many information as possible on CRT
display in general fire fighting system and simultaneously, to equip
functions to simulate whole system.
b)   Security  Experience
To provide against emergencies, performance of security experience as
planned and attendance of local experience and liaison association are most
important.   It is expected that  regular  performance  of  experience   and
education about skill of facilities operation such as physical properties
of LNG, equipments, facilities and structure and information & exercise
on  fire  extinguish  are   desirable.           Moreover,   fire   fighting
organization and communication network according to the size of calamity
and the occured places ( inside factory, vessel and free standing piled
structure ) and practical experience are stated as below.
(1) Fire Extinguish Exercise
Prompt fire extinguish by powdered fire extinguish equipment and by
the combination of water curtain and powdered fire extinguish and valve
operation by water curtain protection, how to approach to fire in case of
using water curtain should be exercised regularly as planned.       In  this
case, it is effective to give change on the alteration of fire size and
magnification and to make gas liquids and complex fire sources appeared.
(2) Imaginary Exercise
Plan imaginary impacts and make an order or report by controlling
counter measures and operation.
(3) Arranngement Exercise
Acquire swift and precise activity on water disposal, valve operation
as soon as a fire had occurred.
(4) Command Transfer Exercise
Commanders make an order based on well-defined status and officers
transfer the commands by oral or wireless phone.
-400 -



(5) Fire Hose Replacement Exercise
In the case of long-last fire, fire hose replacement during
continuous water ejection  will  be  carried  out.     It  is  important  to
establish a better fire protection system to not only increase qulitative
level but also perform regular and general exercise to provide sufficient
activity of terminal fire-protection.
-401-

Reviewing population tendency of Incheon city where the project site
belongs to, populations in Incheon city are on an increasing trend

households are investigated as 126,801  households   in  1970.       243,625
households in 1980 and 455,610 households in 1989.   On   the other   hands,
population  density  has  been  decreased   due   to    the   expansion   of
administrative district since 1988. which   is  6,713  person/kg   in  1984.
7,757.4 persons/kd in 1988 and 5,598 persons/kg in 1989.

B. Environmental Impacts by Project
Based on the city planning of Incheon city, circumferencial area of
the project site is planned to be reclaimed and hence, population will be
increased during the process of construction due to moved-in workers and 70
persons for operation, 85 persons for maintenance, 145 persons for
management & administration of total 300 persons as stated in table 5.3.1 -
5 will be inhabited after the completion of the project,    however,  it  is
expected that the movement of population owing to this project is
negligible.

5.3.2 Industries
A.  Present  Environment  Condition
Status of population for economical activities and employee by each
industries are the facts to indicate characteristics of the districts and
economical activities of the residence precisely.     Industrial  tendencies
of Incheon city is as follows.     The absolute value of primary 'industries
is going to be increased because farm lands are expected to be expanded
finally by the large scaled reclamation project even city development
planning in the future will cause the reduction of farm land though and the
improvement of enterprise management brings development of fisheries,
however, primary industries will be gradually decreased.
Intellectual information industries and social indirect capital and
service  business  respect  to  export  trading   has  brought  changes   to
agriculture and  fisheries  but  there   is a   growing  tendency  that  the
-405-



secondary industries are being shown the steady development forming
industrial complex as industrial city of consumption, whereas primary and
tertiary industries are weakening gradually.
On the other hands, status of empolee by each industries of Incheon
city has been revealed that 17,541 persons are engaged in agriculture and
fisheries and 232,452 persons are in mining and manufacturing industries
and 280,847 persons are with social indirect capital and service business.
Participation rate of economical activities is 50.4 % which is less
than 53.7 % of national participation rate of economical activities and
furthermore, unemployment rate is 3.6 % which is much higher than national
unemployment rate of 2.8 %.

B. Environmental Impacts by Project
Impacts on the industrial structure of Incheon city by this project are
considered to be slight and negligible, however, it is expected that
industries  related  to  LNG   will  be  developed  rapidly,      since  the
increasing  demand  can  be   satisfied.     Also,  LNG  as  an  generalized
industrial energy with the exception of electricity generation, home
cooking, fuel is expected not only to increase usage demand for the energy
of a large boiler, incinerator, reactor of an integrated iron and steel
mill and chemical plant on the point of view that can solve S02 problems
which produced unconditionally from coal or heavy oil energy consumption,
but also to have a worth by utilizing Methane, major composition of LNG, as
a raw material for chemical process.
-408-



And since LNG is an liquids in polar low   temperature   about  -160  oC,
development of industries respect to liquefied separation of air, an ultra
low temperature warehouse, power generation utilizing cold heat are
anticipated by using cold heat effectively that produced from heat exchange
during the process of evaporation and characteristics and kinds of cold
heat industries are as follows.

5.3.3 Public Institutions
Total no.s of public institution of Incheon city is 435 no.s that
local administration government offices are 136 and police & fire stations
are 128 and district court & public prosecutors office are 5 as described
in table 5.3.3 - 1 and in Nam-koo to where the project site belongs, total
107 public institution has been investigated that local administration
government offices are 38, police & fire stations are 30, district court &
public prosecutors offices are 3.
On the other hands, status of a medical institution has revealed that
total 725 hospitals are consists of 10 general hospitals and 7 hospitals
etc., and total 209 hospitals are in Nam-koo.However, rate of the benefits
are only 0.04 % for the total 1,754,376 population of Incheon city and 0.16
% for the 134,671 population in Nam-koo, therefore, regional unbalance for
a medical care has shown between them.
No impacts are evaluated to the public institutions owing to this
project construction.

5.3.5 Transportation
A. Present Environmental Condition
1. Overland Transportation
Urban traffic system of Incheon city are consists of Kyung-in
expressway, Soo-in industrial road as district interconnection road and a
state road which connect to Seoul ( line no.6 & 46   ) and   local  road  to
Kim-po and Gang-hwa( line no. 305 ),   and  Kyung-in  electric  railway  and
Soo-in railroad line are also under service as a railroad.    Also, sealanes
which  connects   Incheon  city  to  circumferencial  islands  ate   already
developed as stated in table 5.3.5 - 1.

electric railway induces cite separation and heavy traffic jam in rush hour
is also becoming an issue like other city, system and orientation of rioaods
are somewhat unreasonable and functional characteristic of the road is
doubted.

increasement of personal transportation system.

According to sea-route status of Incheon city, there are six sea-route
from regular liners from Incheon harbour and Kang-hwa island as a starting
point and among six sea-routes, Incheon to Deock-jeock ( 33 miles ),
Incheon to Young-you ( 15 miles ), Incheon to Dae-boo ( 13 miles ) and
Incheon to Young-heung ( 16 miles ) are regular lines and Incheon to
Young-jong ( 3 miles ), Incheon to Jack-yack island are irregular lines and
hence, total voyage distance is 83 miles and 8 vessels are under service.
Also for voyages to distant islands, 10 vessel liners are traveling 352
miles, 8 sea-routes, under service for marine transportation of commodities
and inhabitants,e.g,Incheon to Back-ryung ( 120 miles ), Incheon to
Yeon-pyung ( 66 miles ), Jin-ri to Wi-do ( 31 miles ), Incheon to Youn-jack

miles ), Joo-moon to Yoi-po ( 18 miles to southern dir. sea-route ),

B. Environmental Impacts by Project
1. Overland Transportation
To evaluate transportation alteration and demand induced by the
project construction, Incheon and Boocheon city has been confined to
minimal administrative districts as a major zone to be investigated taking
consideration of utilization of the data on social and economical prospect
in the future, and other areas are integrated as large scaled outside zone
to encourage efficiency of analysis. ( refer to table 5.3.5 - 10 & Fig.
5.3.5 - 2 )

The most important portion in the process of analyzing traffic demand
is the exact evaluation of future trip  distribution.      Major   important
subject to be treated in the analysis of trip distribution   evaluation   is
to form a relation with given traffics at the destination of each traffic
zone of the area to be investigated and Synthetic Distribution Method has
been utilized for this evaluation,   and model    for  the demand of    trip
distribution prediction has been approached and analyzed by using maximized
Entropy model,    and it   is  expected  that  road construction   plan  for
traffic distribution should be established as described in table 5.3.5 - 6
thru 10 which shows annual increase of traffic   and  in  conclusion,    the
fact that LNG transpotation is performed not by vehicle but by underground
pipe indicates that impacts on traffies due to the LNG receving terminal is
negligible.

On the other hands,   LNG  *vill be planning   to   imported  from Arun
terminal of Indonesia after completion of the project and 3 no.s of 125,000
DWT class carrier vessel will be mobilized for import of 3,000,000 ton/year
and details on above are described as follows.
- No.S of yearly Shipment = 3,000,000/(125,000 x 0.472 x 0.9) = 57
Shipment
- No.S of Req'd Vessel = (57Shipment x 17.5day)/350day = 3 Vessel
* Cycle time per Shipment to Arun Terminal, Indonesia   17.5 days
41Loading : Arunn 1.5 day
X1Round Trip : 14 days
71Unloading and Mooring : 2 days
age distance from carrier vessel to LNG receving terminal is about 44 km
from An-island to Palmi-island as approaching channel and about 4 km from
Palmi-do to ship turning area as entrance channel, and approximately 22.7
hours are required for voyage of above.
Accordingly, harbour possession ratio in the process of annual
3,000,000 ton  unloading  operation  at  the  LNG  receving   terminal    is
evaluated by approximately 19 % and ratio of stand-by time to unloading
operation time by Quenching theory is expected by about 6 % and therefore,
1 Berth is sufficient for annual 3,000,000 ton unloading operation since
stand-by time is quite low.    However in the future,   2 Berth are required
for annual 8,000,000 ton unloading operation based on the characteristics
of process and LNG compositions, and total required no.s of shipment will
be increased to 150 shipments for 2 Berth operation, and harbour possession
ratio is anticipated by 38 % and environmental impacts will not be expected
because of approx.    6 % of ratio of stand-by time to unloading   operation
time by Quenching theory.
C. Method for Reducing the Baneful Impact
The LNG receving terminal is planning to arrive by approaching to ship
turning area along the entrance channel of 3.3 km outside existing channel
near Moo-uei island and thus, minimum 14 m dredged water depth is required
since maximum draft of LNG car-rier vessel which pass through the entrance
channel is 11.02 m, therefore, 18.6 m of dredged water depth and 10,000,000
m3 of dredged earth quantity is planned in this analysis.    Hence,  impacts
on LNG carrier vessel will not be expected to occur after the completion of
the project.
-436-



5.3.6 Cultural Properties
Cultural properties status of Incheon city to where the project
area belongs investigated by totally 27 cultural properties which comprise
7 national cultural properties and 20 local cultural properties. Based on
the type of cultural properties, they can be described that there are
Incheon celadon manufacturing place as historical relics no. 211 and
Dap-dong Catholic Cathedral as historical relic no. 287 and Yeon-hi dong &
Kyung-seo dong of Incheon as infLux area of cranes which are natural
monument no. 257 and Bong-san mask dance as intangible cultutal assets no.
17 and in addition to above, 10 tangible cultural assets among local
cultural properties and human cultural properties are also exist.
In conclusion, no impacts on the cultural properties due to the
project construction are anticipated since there are not to exist any
cultural properties at the project site and circumferencial area.

CHAPTER 6.
THE UNAVOIDABLE BANEFUL IMPACTS
UPON ENVIRONMENT
-441 -






CHAPTER 6. The Unavoidable Baneful Inpacts
upon Environment
6.1   Natural   Environment
For the construction of Incheon LANG receiving terminal, from
dredging of sea route in the shore of Incheon, causeway and reclamation of
the project site, a change in geographical features of the ocean floor      and
the shape of a sea is generated, and from SS (being generated under
dredging   operations)  and    construction   of    shore   protection    under
construction work, partial effect on the ecosystem of the ocean and the
quality of the seawater is ineviatable.
On the other hand, from the decrease in reclaimed land on account of
LNG receiving terminal construction and dredging, decrease in egg-laying
and habitat of oceanic lives is inevitable.

CHAPTER 8.
THE ESTABLISHMENT of ALTERNATIVE
PLAN and EVALUATION
-455 -






CHAPTER      8.   The Establishment of Alternative Plan and
Evaluation
The project site is located near Incheon port, after the analysis for
the conditions of location in Incheon region and required conditions in the
construction of LNG base in this region in order to secure the optimum site
proposed for l,NG receiving terminal, our project team will choose three
places of the proposed site of the subject of investigation.    In addition,
after the operation of the synthetic evaluation from the comparative
analysis for the evaluation of location detaily, our project team, as the
method to choose the optimum site proposed, have chosen and evaluated as
follows.
8.1   The Establishment of Alternative Plan
The most important   factor  among  the  required  conditions  in  the
location of LNG receiving terminal is that ; profitable region to sea route
and the conditions of harbour is region close to the entrance channel of
Incheon port, in due consideration of the depth of water required that LNG
cargo ship needs is
14m, because the region where the depth of water is shallow is reuquired
dredging for the mooring anchorage, place for ship turning and the region
where is required excessive is the worst region on the conditions of
harbor, our project team excepted the region which the depth of water is
shallow and the region which required excessive dredging from the subject
of selection.
So, as taking advantage of the existing sea route and the existing harbor
facilities, to the hightest degree, as much as possible, our project team
has set up three alternatives and the location of three alternatives is the
same as we presented it in fig. 7.1-1.
Meanwhile, the first alternative is that the establishment of a sea
route and a place for ship turning is possible through a small amount of
dredging but since the LNG cargo ship should pass via Inchoen port and the
sea route is complicated and dangerous region. The second alternative is
that the establishment of a sea route and a pLace for ship turning through
a somewhat amount of dredging is possible and good in the safety of a sea
-457-



route but the second alternative is some distant from the land, that is 4.3
km, and is complicated as the first alternative. The third alternative is
very good region in the safety of a sea route and dredging is required to
establish a place for ship turning.    For these three regions, our  project
team has compared and examined as the following (table 8.1-1)

8.2     Evaluation of the Alternative
The conditions of a regional community the nature of coupling on
the back, natural conditions, sea route and the conditions of harbour, etc.
have been analyzed in order to select the most suitable site proposed of
LNG receiving terminal in lncheon.
In the near future, as the harbour district of the region of a new
city on the sea of song island, our project team has adopted the A-3 region
that is excellent in the safety of a sea route.
-461-






CHAPTER 9.
THE COMPREHENSIVE EVALUATION
and CONCLUSION
-463 -






CHAPTER 9. The Comprehensive evaluation and
conclusion
As the construction of Incheon LNG receiving terminal project is
carried out, that will contribute to the enlargement of the national land
especially tideland of no special utility value is transformed into a land,
by making use of this reclaimed land as a site for supply for a place of a
domestic LNG demand.   That will raise the efficiency of   use  of  land  and
will largely contribute to decrease the air pollution in the Metropolitan
area and provide supply for LNG demand.
Consequently, in consideration of an affirmative aspect, the
construction of the project will be desirable but partially negative
impacts which is caused by the construction of the project namly, the
impacts of the environment of the ocean due to the occurrence of earth and
sand from dredging and reclamation, temporary delcine of air quality from
the occurrence of air pollutant under construction, the occurrence of noise
by construction equipment, etc. will[ be accompanied with a baneful impact
upon environment, too.
As a result of analyzing the impact upon natural environment,
living environment and social, economic environment comprehensively by the
construction of this project, the various impact upon environment were
forecasted and, for the partially negative impact, by means of devising a
plan of minimizing it and establishing continuous monitoring system for
the conservation of environment, our project team anticipate that this
project will be proceeded efficiently.
